The binding resource for a pod though may be /pods/foo/binding, which has resource \\\"pods\\\", subresource \\\"binding\\\", and kind \\\"Binding\\\".\\n43: \\tGetSubresource() string\\n44: \\t// GetOperation is the operation being performed\\n45: \\tGetOperation() Operation\\n46: \\t// GetOperationOptions is the options for the operation being performed\\n47: \\tGetOperationOptions() runtime.Object\\n48: \\t// IsDryRun indicates that modifications will definitely not be persisted for this request. \"## Kubernetes API Server Admission Controller Pipeline\\n\\nThe Kubernetes API server admission controller pipeline is a sophisticated system for dynamically intercepting and modifying/validating API requests. The pipeline consists of several interconnected layers:\\n\\n### Core Admission Infrastructure (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\nThe foundation is defined in **interfaces.go**, which provides:\\n- **Interface**: Base interface with `Handles(operation Operation)` method for all admission controllers\\n- **MutationInterface**: Extends Interface with `Admit(ctx context.Context, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error` for mutating admission\\n- **ValidationInterface**: Extends Interface with `Validate(ctx context.Context, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error` for validating admission\\n- **Attributes**: Request metadata interface with methods like `GetName()`, `GetNamespace()`, `GetObject()`, `GetOldObject()`, `GetOperation()`, `GetUserInfo()`, and annotation methods\\n- **ObjectInterfaces**: Interface for object manipulation providing converters, defaulters, and type information\\n\\nThe **Handler** (handler.go) provides a base class for admission plugins, storing which operations (CREATE, UPDATE, DELETE, CONNECT) a plugin handles, with `NewHandler()` for creation.\\n\\n### Chain Execution (chain.go)\\n\\nThe **chainAdmissionHandler** is a slice of `Interface` objects that executes admission plugins in order:\\n- `NewChainHandler()` creates a chain from multiple handlers\\n- `Admit()` iterates through handlers calling `Admit()` on each MutationInterface, returning immediately on error\\n- `Validate()` iterates through handlers calling `Validate()` on each ValidationInterface, returning immediately on error\\n- `Handles()` returns true if any handler handles the operation\\n\\n### Plugin Registration and Initialization (plugins.go)\\n\\nThe **Plugins** registry manages all admission plugins:\\n- `Register()` registers a Factory function by plugin name\\n- `NewFromPlugins()` instantiates plugins from a list of names, wraps them with decorators, and creates a reinvocation handler around a chain\\n- `InitPlugin()` creates a single plugin instance and calls `ValidateInitialization()` on it\\n\\nThe **server/plugins.go** file provides `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()` which registers all default plugins including ValidatingAdmissionWebhook, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, and ValidatingAdmissionPolicy.\\n\\n### Reinvocation Handler (reinvocation.go)\\n\\nThe **reinvoker** wraps the admission chain to support webhook reinvocation policies:\\n- `newReinvocationHandler()` creates the wrapper\\n- `Admit()` executes the chain and may re-execute if a webhook sets `ShouldReinvoke()`\\n- `Validate()` simply delegates to the wrapped chain's ValidationInterface\\n\\n### Mutating Admission Webhooks\\n\\n**Mutating webhook plugin** (plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go):\\n- Implements `MutationInterface` and `admission.Interface`\\n- `NewMutatingWebhook()` creates a plugin with a generic webhook infrastructure\\n- `Admit()` delegates to `Webhook.Dispatch()` for calling remote webhooks\\n\\n**Mutating webhook configuration manager** (configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go):\\n- **mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration resources\\n- `NewMutatingWebhookConfigurationManager()` creates the manager with an informer\\n- `getMutatingWebhookConfigurations()` orders webhook configurations deterministically by name (line 121: `sort.SliceStable(configurations, MutatingWebhookConfigurationSorter(configurations).ByName)`) and creates WebhookAccessor objects with caching\\n- `Webhooks()` returns merged webhook accessors\\n\\n**Mutating webhook dispatcher** (plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go):\\n- **mutatingDispatcher** handles the execution of mutating webhooks\\n- `Dispatch()` iterates through webhooks, calling each one and applying patches to the request object\\n- Supports reinvocation based on object changes\\n\\n### Validating Admission Webhooks\\n\\n**Validating webhook plugin** (plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go):\\n- Implements `ValidationInterface` and `admission.Interface`\\n- `NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook()` creates a plugin with generic webhook infrastructure\\n- `Validate()` delegates to `Webhook.Dispatch()` for calling remote webhooks\\n\\n**Validating webhook configuration manager** (configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go):\\n- **validatingWebhookConfigurationManager** watches ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources\\n- `NewValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager()` creates the manager with an informer\\n- `getValidatingWebhookConfigurations()` orders configurations by name and creates WebhookAccessor objects\\n- Caches webhook accessors to avoid recompilation of CEL expressions\\n\\n**Validating webhook dispatcher** (plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go):\\n- **validatingDispatcher** executes validating webhooks in parallel where possible\\n- `Dispatch()` constructs versioned attributes for each webhook and calls them\\n- Returns immediately on first validation error\\n\\n### Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\n**Generic webhook** (plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go):\\n- **Webhook** struct provides common infrastructure for both mutating and validating webhooks\\n- `NewWebhook()` initializes the webhook with client managers, namespace/object matchers, and a dispatcher\\n- Handles authentication, timeout, and other common webhook concerns\\n\\n**Webhook accessors** (plugin/webhook/accessors.go):\\n- **WebhookAccessor** interface provides a common way to access mutating and validating webhook configurations\\n- `NewMutatingWebhookAccessor()` creates accessors for MutatingWebhook objects\\n- Accessors provide lazy initialization of client connections, namespace/object selectors, and compiled match conditions\\n\\n### Kubernetes-specific Admission\\n\\n- **pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go**: Kubernetes-specific admission plugin options and ordering\\n- **pkg/controlplane/apiserver/samples/generic/server/admission.go**: Sample setup showing how admission plugins are initialized with default ordering\\n\\n## Execution Flow\\n\\n1. API request arrives at the server\\n2. Reinvocation handler wraps the request\\n3. Mutating admission chain executes in order:\\n   - MutatingAdmissionPolicy plugins\\n   - MutatingAdmissionWebhook plugins (which call remote webhooks in serial, applying patches)\\n   - Other mutating plugins (ResourceQuota, etc.)\\n4. Validating admission chain executes in order:\\n   - ValidatingAdmissionPolicy plugins\\n   - ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugins (which call remote webhooks in parallel)\\n   - Other validating plugins\\n5. If reinvocation is needed, the entire chain may execute again\\n6. Request either proceeds to storage or is rejected with error\\n\\nThe webhook ordering is deterministic by sorting configurations by name, ensuring consistent behavior across API server instances.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":13,"cache_creation_input_tokens":4869,"cache_read_input_tokens":109198,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":4869},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"2c272d6a-e734-4022-8ad8-272f669b6632","uuid":"3e0e7426-7d96-4acc-b5c6-bf1f3b4b3fd3"}

\"## Kubernetes API Server Admission Controller Pipeline\\n\\nThe Kubernetes API server admission controller pipeline is a sophisticated system for dynamically intercepting and modifying/validating API requests. The pipeline consists of several interconnected layers:\\n\\n### Core Admission Infrastructure (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\nThe foundation is defined in **interfaces.go**, which provides:\\n- **Interface**: Base interface with `Handles(operation Operation)` method for all admission controllers\\n- **MutationInterface**: Extends Interface with `Admit(ctx context.Context, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error` for mutating admission\\n- **ValidationInterface**: Extends Interface with `Validate(ctx context.Context, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error` for validating admission\\n- **Attributes**: Request metadata interface with methods like `GetName()`, `GetNamespace()`, `GetObject()`, `GetOldObject()`, `GetOperation()`, `GetUserInfo()`, and annotation methods\\n- **ObjectInterfaces**: Interface for object manipulation providing converters, defaulters, and type information\\n\\nThe **Handler** (handler.go) provides a base class for admission plugins, storing which operations (CREATE, UPDATE, DELETE, CONNECT) a plugin handles, with `NewHandler()` for creation.\\n\\n### Chain Execution (chain.go)\\n\\nThe **chainAdmissionHandler** is a slice of `Interface` objects that executes admission plugins in order:\\n- `NewChainHandler()` creates a chain from multiple handlers\\n- `Admit()` iterates through handlers calling `Admit()` on each MutationInterface, returning immediately on error\\n- `Validate()` iterates through handlers calling `Validate()` on each ValidationInterface, returning immediately on error\\n- `Handles()` returns true if any handler handles the operation\\n\\n### Plugin Registration and Initialization (plugins.go)\\n\\nThe **Plugins** registry manages all admission plugins:\\n- `Register()` registers a Factory function by plugin name\\n- `NewFromPlugins()` instantiates plugins from a list of names, wraps them with decorators, and creates a reinvocation handler around a chain\\n- `InitPlugin()` creates a single plugin instance and calls `ValidateInitialization()` on it\\n\\nThe **server/plugins.go** file provides `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()` which registers all default plugins including ValidatingAdmissionWebhook, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, and ValidatingAdmissionPolicy.\\n\\n### Reinvocation Handler (reinvocation.go)\\n\\nThe **reinvoker** wraps the admission chain to support webhook reinvocation policies:\\n- `newReinvocationHandler()` creates the wrapper\\n- `Admit()` executes the chain and may re-execute if a webhook sets `ShouldReinvoke()`\\n- `Validate()` simply delegates to the wrapped chain's ValidationInterface\\n\\n### Mutating Admission Webhooks\\n\\n**Mutating webhook plugin** (plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go):\\n- Implements `MutationInterface` and `admission.Interface`\\n- `NewMutatingWebhook()` creates a plugin with a generic webhook infrastructure\\n- `Admit()` delegates to `Webhook.Dispatch()` for calling remote webhooks\\n\\n**Mutating webhook configuration manager** (configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go):\\n- **mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration resources\\n- `NewMutatingWebhookConfigurationManager()` creates the manager with an informer\\n- `getMutatingWebhookConfigurations()` orders webhook configurations deterministically by name (line 121: `sort.SliceStable(configurations, MutatingWebhookConfigurationSorter(configurations).ByName)`) and creates WebhookAccessor objects with caching\\n- `Webhooks()` returns merged webhook accessors\\n\\n**Mutating webhook dispatcher** (plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go):\\n- **mutatingDispatcher** handles the execution of mutating webhooks\\n- `Dispatch()` iterates through webhooks, calling each one and applying patches to the request object\\n- Supports reinvocation based on object changes\\n\\n### Validating Admission Webhooks\\n\\n**Validating webhook plugin** (plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go):\\n- Implements `ValidationInterface` and `admission.Interface`\\n- `NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook()` creates a plugin with generic webhook infrastructure\\n- `Validate()` delegates to `Webhook.Dispatch()` for calling remote webhooks\\n\\n**Validating webhook configuration manager** (configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go):\\n- **validatingWebhookConfigurationManager** watches ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources\\n- `NewValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager()` creates the manager with an informer\\n- `getValidatingWebhookConfigurations()` orders configurations by name and creates WebhookAccessor objects\\n- Caches webhook accessors to avoid recompilation of CEL expressions\\n\\n**Validating webhook dispatcher** (plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go):\\n- **validatingDispatcher** executes validating webhooks in parallel where possible\\n- `Dispatch()` constructs versioned attributes for each webhook and calls them\\n- Returns immediately on first validation error\\n\\n### Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\n**Generic webhook** (plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go):\\n- **Webhook** struct provides common infrastructure for both mutating and validating webhooks\\n- `NewWebhook()` initializes the webhook with client managers, namespace/object matchers, and a dispatcher\\n- Handles authentication, timeout, and other common webhook concerns\\n\\n**Webhook accessors** (plugin/webhook/accessors.go):\\n- **WebhookAccessor** interface provides a common way to access mutating and validating webhook configurations\\n- `NewMutatingWebhookAccessor()` creates accessors for MutatingWebhook objects\\n- Accessors provide lazy initialization of client connections, namespace/object selectors, and compiled match conditions\\n\\n### Kubernetes-specific Admission\\n\\n- **pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go**: Kubernetes-specific admission plugin options and ordering\\n- **pkg/controlplane/apiserver/samples/generic/server/admission.go**: Sample setup showing how admission plugins are initialized with default ordering\\n\\n## Execution Flow\\n\\n1. API request arrives at the server\\n2. Reinvocation handler wraps the request\\n3. Mutating admission chain executes in order:\\n   - MutatingAdmissionPolicy plugins\\n   - MutatingAdmissionWebhook plugins (which call remote webhooks in serial, applying patches)\\n   - Other mutating plugins (ResourceQuota, etc.)\\n4. Validating admission chain executes in order:\\n   - ValidatingAdmissionPolicy plugins\\n   - ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugins (which call remote webhooks in parallel)\\n   - Other validating plugins\\n5. If reinvocation is needed, the entire chain may execute again\\n6. Request either proceeds to storage or is rejected with error\\n\\nThe webhook ordering is deterministic by sorting configurations by name, ensuring consistent behavior across API server instances.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
